(define *testdirs* (system-output (format #f "ls -d /net/seykhl/aux/sbroniko/vader-rover/logs/house-test-12nov15/~a*" "floorplan-0")))

(define *gm-vars*
	 (join (map (lambda (dir) (get-graphical-model-variables dir)) *testdirs*)))

(define *snl* (find-same-nouns *gm-vars*))

(define *noun-list* (map first *gm-vars*))

(define *all-tubes* (join (map (lambda (dir) (find-low-variance-tubes dir)) *testdirs*))) 

(define *few-tubes* (sublist (removeq #f *all-tubes*) 0 5))

(define *ra* (join (map (lambda (d) (third (read-object-from-file (format #f "~a/alignment.sc" d)))) *testdirs*)))

(define *hnl* (make-helper-noun-list *ra*))

(define *tube1* (first *few-tubes*))

(define *tube2* (second *few-tubes*))

(define *pos1* (subvector (first (first *tube1*)) 0 2))

(define *pos2* (subvector (first (first *tube2*)) 0 2))
(define *nnbs* (find-noun-noun-binary-score-matrix *all-tubes* (first *hnl*)))
(define *hnbs-list* (map (lambda (l) (find-noun-noun-binary-score-matrix *few-tubes* l)) *hnl*))
(define *videos-list* (remove-duplicates (map third (removeq #f *all-tubes*))))
(define *video-frames*  (map (lambda (v) (video->frames 1 v)) *videos-list*))
